39        public void test001() {
40                this.runNegativeTest(
41                        new String[] {
42                                "Y.java",
43                                "public class Y<T> extends X<A> { public void foo(T t) {} }\n" +
44                                "class X<U> { public void foo(U u) {} }\n" +
45                                "class A {}\n"
46                        },
47                        "----------\n" + 
48                        "1. ERROR in Y.java (at line 1)\n" + 
49                        "        public class Y<T> extends X<A> { public void foo(T t) {} }\n" + 
50                        "                                                     ^^^^^^^^\n" + 
51                        "Name clash: The method foo(T) of type Y<T> has the same erasure as foo(U) of type X<U> but does not override it\n" + 
52                        "----------\n"
53                        // name clash: foo(T) in Y<T> and foo(U) in X<A> have the same erasure, yet neither overrides the other
54                );
55        }

663                        W.java:1: incompatible types
664                        found   : java.lang.Object
665                        required: T
666                        class W<T> extends X { public T foo() { return super.foo(); } }
667                        Y.java:1: foo() in Y cannot override foo() in X; attempting to use incompatible return type
668                        Y.java:1: incompatible types
669                        found   : A
670                        required: T
671                        class Y<T> extends X<A> { public T foo() { return super.foo(); } }
672                         */
673                        null,
674                        false,
675                        null
676                );
677        }

859                                "        System.out.print(\" + \");\n" +
860                                "        I i = new A();\n" +
861                                "        i.foo();\n" +
862                                "    }\n" +
863                                "}\n" +

865                                "    public I foo();\n" +
866                                "}\n" +
867                                "class A extends X implements I {\n" +
868                                "    public A foo() {\n" +
869                                "        System.out.print(\"Added bridge method\");\n" +
870                                "        return this;\n" +
871                                "    }\n" +
872                                "}\n"
873                        },
874                        "Added bridge method + Added bridge method"
875                );
876        }

7106public void test114() {
7107        Map options = this.getCompilerOptions();
7108        options.put(CompilerOptions.OPTION_ReportOverridingMethodWithoutSuperInvocation, CompilerOptions.ERROR);
7109        this.runNegativeTest(
7110                new String[] {
7111                        "X.java",
7112                        "class Y {\n" + 
7113                        "  void foo() {}\n" + 
7114                        "}\n" + 
7115                        "public class X extends Y {\n" + 
7116                        "  @Override\n" +
7117                        "  void foo() {\n" + 
7118                        "  }\n" + 
7119                        "}"
7120                },
7121                "----------\n" + 
7122                "1. ERROR in X.java (at line 6)\n" + 
7123                "        void foo() {\n" + 
7124                "             ^^^^^\n" + 
7125                "The method X.foo() is overriding a method without making a super invocation\n" + 
7126                "----------\n",
7127                null,
7128                true,
7129                options
7130        );
7131}

7158public void test116() {
7159           Map options = this.getCompilerOptions();
7160           options.put(CompilerOptions.OPTION_ReportOverridingMethodWithoutSuperInvocation, CompilerOptions.ERROR);
7161        String expectedOutput = new CompilerOptions(options).sourceLevel < ClassFileConstants.JDK1_6
7162        ?        "----------\n" + 
7163                "1. ERROR in X.java (at line 2)\n" + 
7164                "        Zork foo() {}\n" + 
7165                "        ^^^^\n" + 
7166                "Zork cannot be resolved to a type\n" + 
7167                "----------\n" + 
7168                "2. ERROR in X.java (at line 6)\n" + 
7169                "        Object foo() {\n" + 
7170                "               ^^^^^\n" + 
7171                "The method foo() of type X must override a superclass method\n" + 
7172                "----------\n"
7173        :        "----------\n" + 
7174                "1. ERROR in X.java (at line 2)\n" + 
7175                "        Zork foo() {}\n" + 
7176                "        ^^^^\n" +
